Overview

HTTP status codes

Scoring Engine uses following HTTP status codes.

Status code Usage

200 OK

The request completed successfully.

201 Created

A new resource has been created successfully. The resource’s URI is available from the response’s Location header.

204 No Content

A deletion of an existing resource has been applied successfully

400 Bad Request

The request was malformed. The response body will include an error providing further information.

401 Unauthorized

The request has not been applied because it lacks valid authentication credentials for the target resource.

404 Not Found

The requested resource did not exist.

409 Conflict

Indicates that the request could not be processed because of conflict in the request, such as creation new resource with id already existing one.

422 Unprocessable Entity

The request was well-formed but was unable to be followed due to semantic errors.

Resources

Scenario

The Scenario resource is used to manage scenarios.

Importing scenarios

A POST request is used to import scenarios.

Request structure

Headers
Name Description

Authorization

Authorization token
Parameters
Parameter Description

overwrite

Indicates if overwrite existing scenarios with the same name

Example request

$ curl 'http://example.org/api/scenario/import?overwrite=false' -i -X POST -H 'Accept: application/json' -H 'Authorization: Bearer cx0djnmb-zrtz-90j1-whkx-qqktkcahgwsc' -H 'Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8' -d '[ {
  "id" : "5929acd65827d2000734937f",
  "name" : "simple",
  "createdAt" : 1495903446443,
  "updatedAt" : 1495903471971,
  "content" : "{\"cells\":[{\"type\":\"html.Element\",\"position\":{\"x\":378,\"y\":177},\"backendModelParams\":{\"name\":\"Start\",\"id\":\"5929aceb5827d20007349380\",\"entityIdentifier\":\"start\"},\"options\":{\"interactive\":true},\"isChartNode\":true,\"id\":\"0e590ebd-41f7-41f9-9748-8e23e6b297ef\",\"z\":1,\"attrs\":{\".name\":{\"text\":\"Start\",\"x\":\"30px\",\"y\":\"24px\",\"x-alignment\":\"left\"},\".full-name\":{\"text\":\"Start\"},\".connection-port\":{\"display\":\"block\"},\".connection-port-true\":{\"display\":\"none\"},\".connection-port-false\":{\"display\":\"none\"},\".connection-port-decision-true\":{\"display\":\"none\"},\".connection-port-decision-false\":{\"display\":\"none\"},\"rect\":{\"fill\":\"#43a047\"}}},{\"type\":\"html.Element\",\"position\":{\"x\":353,\"y\":331},\"backendModelParams\":{\"name\":\"Expression\",\"id\":\"5929aced5827d20007349381\",\"entityIdentifier\":\"expression\"},\"options\":{\"interactive\":true},\"isChartNode\":true,\"id\":\"0bdd89e3-80a8-4f33-89b6-a52ffb631e46\",\"z\":2,\"attrs\":{\".name\":{\"text\":\"Expression\",\"x\":\"30px\",\"y\":\"24px\",\"x-alignment\":\"left\"},\".full-name\":{\"text\":\"Expression\"},\".connection-port\":{\"display\":\"block\"},\".connection-port-true\":{\"display\":\"none\"},\".connection-port-false\":{\"display\":\"none\"},\".connection-port-decision-true\":{\"display\":\"none\"},\".connection-port-decision-false\":{\"display\":\"none\"},\"rect\":{\"fill\":\"#009688\"}}},{\"type\":\"link\",\"source\":{\"id\":\"0e590ebd-41f7-41f9-9748-8e23e6b297ef\"},\"target\":{\"id\":\"0bdd89e3-80a8-4f33-89b6-a52ffb631e46\"},\"backendModelParams\":{\"id\":\"5929acef5827d20007349382\"},\"isChartNode\":false,\"data\":{},\"id\":\"c2428e66-7467-4c3b-a32a-3114b7762e37\",\"z\":3,\"vertices\":[{\"x\":411,\"y\":277.5}],\"attrs\":{\".marker-target\":{\"d\":\"M Creating scenario process

A GET request is used to create scenario process.

Request structure

The request path contains following parameters:

Table 1. /api/scenario/process/create/{scenarioId}
Parameter Description

scenarioId

Scenario id
Headers
Name Description

Authorization

Authorization token

Example request

$ curl 'http://example.org/api/scenario/process/create/5929acd65827d2000734937f' -i -H 'Authorization: Bearer cx0djnmb-zrtz-90j1-whkx-qqktkcahgwsc' -H 'Accept: */*'

Response structure

Response status should be 200 or suitable error will be returned.

Example response

HTTP/1.1 200 OK
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Transfer-Encoding: chunked
Date: Fri, 23 Feb 2018 11:01:34 GMT
Content-Length: 961

{
  "nodes" : {

Code

The Code resource is used to manage codes.

Importing codes

A POST request is used to import codes.

Request structure

Headers
Name Description

Authorization

Authorization token
Parameters
Parameter Description

overwrite

Indicates if overwrite existing codes with the same name

Example request

$ curl 'http://example.org/api/code/import?overwrite=false' -i -X POST -H 'Accept: application/json' -H 'Authorization: Bearer cx0djnmb-zrtz-90j1-whkx-qqktkcahgwsc' -H 'Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8' -d '[ {
  "type" : "scoring",
  "name" : "Simple",
  "className" : "SimpleScoringCode",
  "content" : "package com.ziom;\n\nimport java.util.HashMap;\nimport java.util.Map;\nimport java.util.Set;\nimport pl.algolytics.aengine.scoring.code.interfaces.ScoringCode;\n\nimport static java.util.stream.Collectors.toMap;\n\npublic class SimpleScoringCode implements ScoringCode {\n\n    private static final Map<String, Class> INPUT_ATTRIBUTES = new HashMap<String, Class>() {{\n        put(\"A\", Double.class);\n        put(\"B\", Double.class);\n        put(\"C\", Double.class);        \n    }};\n\n    public Map<String, Double> prepareData(Map<String, Object> inputData) {\n        return inputData.entrySet().stream().collect(toMap(Map.Entry::getKey, e -> checkAndInitializeValue(e.getValue())));\n    }\n\n    private Double checkAndInitializeValue(Object tmpAttr) {\n        if (tmpAttr != null) {\n            if (tmpAttr instanceof Number)\n                return ((Number) tmpAttr).doubleValue();\n            else\n                throw new RuntimeException(\"Data type (\" + tmpAttr.getClass() + \") doesn't match to data type (Number) specified in inputSignature for attribute 'duration'. Can't continue. \");\n        }\n        return Double.NaN;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Map<String, Object> process(HashMap<String, Object> inputData) {\n        return score(prepareData(inputData));\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Map<String, Class> getInputAttributes() {\n        return INPUT_ATTRIBUTES;\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public Set<String> getIds() {\n        return INPUT_ATTRIBUTES.keySet();\n    }\n\n    public Map<String, Object> score(Map<String, Double> inputRow) {\n        Double value = 1d;\n        Map<String, Object> resultMap = new HashMap<>();\n        resultMap.put(\"computeValue\", value);\n        return resultMap;\n    }\n}",
  "data" : null,
  "validFrom" : "2017-05-29",
  "validTo" : "2017-05-29",
  "userId" : "admin",
  "version" : 1,
  "selected" : false
} ]'

Response structure

Response status should be 200 or suitable error will be returned.

Example response

HTTP/1.1 200 OK
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Transfer-Encoding: chunked
Date: Fri, 23 Feb 2018 11:01:35 GMT
Content-Length: 17

{
  "count" : 1
}

Scenario Code

A POST request is used to create a new scenario code.

Request structure

Headers
Name Description

Authorization

Authorization token
Parameters
Parameter Description

name

Scenario code name

increaseVersion

Indicates if increase scenario code version
Body

Body should contain correct json scenario code encoded in plain text.

Example request

$ curl 'http://example.org/api/scenario/code/create?name=simple&increaseVersion=false' -i -X POST -H 'Accept: application/json' -H 'Authorization: Bearer cx0djnmb-zrtz-90j1-whkx-qqktkcahgwsc' -H 'Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8' -d '{
  "nodes" : {
    "1" : {
      "resultPrefix" : null,
      "resultMergeStrategy" : "OVERWRITE_NULL",
      "id" : "1",
      "type" : "START",

        "AAA" : {
          "name" : "AAA",
          "type" : {
            "type" : "INTEGER"
          },
          "required" : true,
          "description" : "",
          "tags" : [ ]
        }
      },
      "variableValidator" : {
        "AAA" : [ {
          "type" : "VARIABLE_TYPE",

Scoring async a scenario code

A Post request is used to score async specified scenario code.

Request structure

The request path contains following parameters:

Table 2. /api/scenario/code/scoreasync/{name}
Parameter Description

name

Scenario code name
Headers
Name Description

Authorization

Authorization token

X-SCE-RequestId

Unique id to identify scoring

X-SCE-CallbackUrl

Callback address to send scoring results

X-SCE-CallbackRetryCount

Callback retry number (if sending scoring results failed)

X-SCE-CallbackRetryDelay

Delay between consecutive callback retries (in seconds)

Example request

$ curl 'http://example.org/api/scenario/code/scoreasync/simple' -i -X POST -H 'Accept: application/json' -H 'Authorization: Bearer cx0djnmb-zrtz-90j1-whkx-qqktkcahgwsc' -H 'X-SCE-RequestId: id_1' -H 'X-SCE-CallbackUrl: http://example.org/' -H 'X-SCE-CallbackRetryCount: 3' -H 'X-SCE-CallbackRetryDelay: 30' -H 'Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8' -d '{
  "AAA" : 2.5
}'

Response structure

Response status should be 200 or suitable error will be returned.

Example response

HTTP/1.1 200 OK
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache

Uploading a scoring code

A POST request is used to upload a scoring code.

Request structure

Parts
Part Description

dateFrom

Date from

dateTo

Date to

fileName

Name of the file, from which we upload scoring code

scoringCodeName

Scoring code name

charset

File encoding

file

File from which we upload scoring code
Headers
Name Description

Authorization

Authorization token

Content-Type

Media type of the resource

Example request

$ curl 'http://example.org/api/scoring/code/create' -i -X POST -H 'Authorization: Bearer tbxsxiel-5flc-97ad-kqc1-ilcjzuc5zs44' -H 'Accept: */*' -H 'Content-Type: multipart/form-data' -F 'dateFrom=@file;type=text/plain' -F 'dateTo=@file;type=text/plain' -F 'fileName=@file;type=text/plain' -F 'scoringCodeName=@file;type=text/plain' -F 'charset=@file;type=text/plain' -F 'file=@testCode.java;type=text/x-java'

Response structure

Response status should be 200 or suitable error will be returned.

}

Deleting a scoring code

A POST request is used to delete a scoring code.

Request structure

Table 8. /api/scoring/code/delete/{name}
Parameter Description

name

Scoring code name
Headers
Name Description

Authorization

Authorization token

Example request

$ curl 'http://example.org/api/scoring/code/delete/Simple' -i -X DELETE -H 'Authorization: Bearer ed4n7nnd-bvaj-vdxc-z9ne-uiqvbesnyklm' -H 'Accept: */*'

Response structure

Response status should be 200 or suitable error will be returned.

Example response

HTTP/1.1 200 OK
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Date: Fri, 23 Feb 2018 11:01:35 GMT

R Code

The R Code resource is used to manage R codes.

Uploading an r code

A POST request is used to upload an r code.

Request structure

Parts
Part Description

dateFrom

Date from

dateTo

Date to

fileName

Name of the file, from which we upload scoring code

rCodeName

r code name

file

File from which we upload scoring code
Headers
Name Description

Authorization

Authorization token

Content-Type

Media type of the resource

Example request

$ curl 'http://example.org/api/r/code/create' -i -X POST -H 'Authorization: Bearer fkudxja9-nla5-c8lm-dxgp-wycltbnf42pp' -H 'Accept: */*' -H 'Content-Type: multipart/form-data' -F 'dateFrom=@file;type=text/plain' -F 'dateTo=@file;type=text/plain' -F 'fileName=@file;type=text/plain' -F 'rCodeName=@file;type=text/plain' -F 'file=@rCodeTest.zip;type=application/zip'

Response structure

Response status should be 200 or suitable error will be returned.

Example response

HTTP/1.1 200 OK
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Date: Fri, 23 Feb 2018 11:01:32 GMT

Getting an r code attributes

A GET request is used to get specified r code attributes.

Request structure

The request path contains following parameters:

Table 10. /api/r/code/attributes/{name}
Parameter Description

name

Scenario code name
Headers
Name Description

Authorization

Authorization token

Example request

$ curl 'http://example.org/api/r/code/attributes/rCodeTestSetup' -i -H 'Authorization: Bearer pudanhaj-wv50-ee0u-olvf-fuoisbvoxxol' -H 'Accept: */*'

Response structure

Response status should be 200 or suitable error will be returned.

Example response

HTTP/1.1 200 OK
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Transfer-Encoding: chunked
Date: Fri, 23 Feb 2018 11:01:32 GMT
Content-Length: 226

{
  "inputAttributesVariable" : {
    "var3" : {
      "type" : "DOUBLE",
      "description" : ""
    },
    "var4" : {
      "type" : "DICTIONARY",
      "options" : [ "aa", "bb", "cc" ],
      "description" : ""
    }
  }
}

Getting an r code list

A Get request is used to get a list of R codes.

Request structure

Headers
Name Description

Authorization

Authorization token

Example request

$ curl 'http://example.org/api/r/code/list' -i -H 'Authorization: Bearer rv2mpzx3-eapt-wueb-njkl-58k0f0tnoakd' -H 'Accept: */*'

Response structure

Response status should be 200 or suitable error will be returned.

Example response

HTTP/1.1 200 OK
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Transfer-Encoding: chunked
Date: Fri, 23 Feb 2018 11:01:32 GMT
Content-Length: 263

[ {
  "id" : "6029acd65827d2000734937f",
  "name" : "rCodeTestSetup",
  "content" : null,
  "variables" : null,
  "rdataContent" : null,
  "rdataType" : null,
  "validFrom" : null,
  "validTo" : null,
  "userId" : null,
  "version" : null,
  "selected" : null
} ]

Downloading an r code

A GET request is used to download specified r code source.

Request structure

The request path contains following parameters:

Table 11. /api/r/code/download/{name}
Parameter Description

name

R code name
Headers
Name Description

Authorization

Authorization token

Example request

$ curl 'http://example.org/api/r/code/download/rCodeTestSetup' -i -H 'Authorization: Bearer gizedndt-k1l9-g6nj-9ijs-6awwudn7yz4v' -H 'Accept: */*'

Response structure

Response status should be 200 or suitable error will be returned.

Deleting an r code

A POST request is used to delete r code.

Request structure

Table 12. /api/r/code/delete/{name}
Parameter Description

name

Scoring code name
Headers
Name Description

Authorization

Authorization token

Example request

$ curl 'http://example.org/api/r/code/delete/rCodeTestSetup' -i -X DELETE -H 'Authorization: Bearer zyrmfkqz-01ct-ud1j-rzc2-cxuvdoqgcgk8' -H 'Accept: */*'

Response structure

Response status should be 200 or suitable error will be returned.

Example response

HTTP/1.1 200 OK
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Date: Fri, 23 Feb 2018 11:01:32 GMT

Pmml Code

The Pmml Code resource is used to manage Pmml codes.

Uploading a pmml code

A POST request is used to upload an pmml code.

Request structure

Parts
Part Description

dateFrom

Date from

dateTo

Date to

fileName

Name of the file, from which we upload pmml code

scoringCodeName

Pmml code name

charset

File encoding

file

File from which we upload pmml code
Headers
Name Description

Authorization

Authorization token

Content-Type

Media type of the resource

Example request

$ curl 'http://example.org/api/pmml/code/create' -i -X POST -H 'Authorization: Bearer z59eyda3-vyog-38qr-zpoz-zwqzafff6dzb' -H 'Accept: */*' -H 'Content-Type: multipart/form-data' -F 'dateFrom=@file;type=text/plain' -F 'dateTo=@file;type=text/plain' -F 'fileName=@file;type=text/plain' -F 'scoringCodeName=@file;type=text/plain' -F 'charset=@file;type=text/plain' -F 'file=@pmmlTest.pmml;type=application/xml'

Response structure

Response status should be 200 or suitable error will be returned.

Example response

HTTP/1.1 200 OK
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Date: Fri, 23 Feb 2018 11:01:32 GMT

Scoring a pmml code

A POST request is used to score specified pmml code.

Request structure

Parameter Description

name

Pmml code name
Headers
Name Description

Authorization

Authorization token

Example request

$ curl 'http://example.org/api/pmml/code/score?name=pmmlTest' -i -X POST -H 'Accept: application/json' -H 'Authorization: Bearer waadtdfi-gqhw-pdlr-xuuy-6rcvypndxfta' -H 'Content-Type: application/json; charset=UTF-8' -d '{
  "Petal_Length" : 1,
  "Petal_Width" : 2,
  "Sepal_Length" : 3,
  "Sepal_Width" : 4
}'

Response structure

Response status should be 200 or suitable error will be returned.

Example response

HTTP/1.1 200 OK
X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff
X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block
Cache-Control: no-cache, no-store, max-age=0, must-revalidate
Pragma: no-cache
Expires: 0
X-Frame-Options: DENY
Content-Type: application/json;charset=UTF-8
Transfer-Encoding: chunked
Date: Fri, 23 Feb 2018 11:01:32 GMT
Content-Length: 444

{
  "name" : "pmmlTest",
  "beginTime" : "2018-02-23T11:01:32.673Z",
  "endTime" : "2018-02-23T11:01:32.773Z",
  "result" : {
    "result" : "virginica",
    "Predicted_Species" : "virginica",
    "Probability_setosa" : 0.0,
    "Probability_versicolor" : 0.021739130434782608,
    "Probability_virginica" : 0.9782608695652174,
    "Petal_Length" : 1,
    "Petal_Width" : 2,
    "Sepal_Length" : 3,
    "Sepal_Width" : 4
  },
  "error" : null
}

Exporting a pmml code

A GET request is used to get specified pmml code in JSON format. The same format is used while importing codes.

Request structure

The request path contains following parameters:

Table 13. /api/pmml/code/get/{name}
Parameter Description

name

Pmml code name
Headers
Name Description

Authorization

Authorization token

Example request

$ curl 'http://example.org/api/pmml/code/get/pmmlTest' -i -H 'Authorization: Bearer xko8ukdh-ptnf-nbtg-c5lj-6z8ysjqjyvug' -H 'Accept: */*'

Response structure

Response status should be 200 or suitable error will be returned.
